<script type="text/javascript">
var CartPerf = (function() {
  var _hasUedata = (typeof uet == 'function');
  var _startedLoading = false;

  var loading = function() {
    if (!_startedLoading && _isReportingEvents()) {
      uet('cb');
    }
    _startedLoading = true;
  };

  var aboveTheFoldLoaded = function() {
    if (_startedLoading && _isReportingEvents()) {
      uet('af');
    }
  };

  var functionalLoaded = function() {
    if (_startedLoading && _isReportingEvents()) {
      uet('fn');
    }
  };

  var criticalFeatureLoaded = function() {
    if (_startedLoading && _isReportingEvents()) {
      uet('cf');
    }
  };

  var x1Loaded = function () {
    if (_startedLoading && _isReportingEvents()) {
      uet('x1');
    }
  }

  var _isReportingEvents = function() {
    return _hasUedata;
  };

  var _hasUEForAJAXRequest = (typeof ues == 'function') && (typeof uex == 'function');
  var _actionNumber = 0;
  var _scope = "cart-ajax";

  var getScope = function() {
    return _scope;
  }

  var resetUEForAJAXRequest = function() {
    _actionNumber++;
    _scope = "cart-ajax-" + _actionNumber;
    if (window.ue && _hasUedata && _hasUEForAJAXRequest) {
      uet("tc", _scope);         // set time-of-click
      ues("ctb", _scope, "1");   // set ctb flag
    }
  }

  // set start time
  var setStartTimeForAJAXRequest = function() {
    if (window.ue && _hasUedata && _hasUEForAJAXRequest) {
      ues("t0", _scope, new Date());
    }
  }

  // set request ID
  var setIDForAJAXRequest = function(rid) {
    if (window.ue && _hasUedata && _hasUEForAJAXRequest) {
      ues("id", _scope, rid);
    }
  }

  // record the event of critical feature loaded
  var cfLoadedForAJAXRequest = function() {
    if (window.ue && _hasUedata && _hasUEForAJAXRequest) {
      uet("cf", _scope);
    }
  }
  
  var atfLoadedForAJAXRequest = function() {
    if (window.ue && _hasUedata && _hasUEForAJAXRequest) {
      uet("af", _scope);
    }
  }

  var fnLoadedForAJAXRequest = function() {
    if (window.ue && _hasUedata && _hasUEForAJAXRequest) {
      uet("fn", _scope);
    }
  }

  // record the event of page loaded
  var pageLoadedForAJAXRequest = function(scope) {
    if (window.ue && _hasUedata && _hasUEForAJAXRequest) {
      if (scope != null) {
        uex("ld", scope);
      } else {
        uex("ld", _scope);
      }
    }
  }
  
  var x1LoadedForAJAXRequest = function() {
    if (window.ue && _hasUedata && _hasUEForAJAXRequest) {
      uet("x1", _scope);
    }
  }

  var x2LoadedForAJAXRequest = function() {
    if (window.ue && _hasUedata && _hasUEForAJAXRequest) {
      uet("x2", _scope);
    }
  }

  var x3LoadedForAJAXRequest = function() {
    if (window.ue && _hasUedata && _hasUEForAJAXRequest) {
      uet("x3", _scope);
    }
  }

  var x2Loaded = function () {
    if (_startedLoading && _isReportingEvents()) {
      uet('x2');
    }
  }

  var x3Loaded = function () {
    if (_startedLoading && _isReportingEvents()) {
      uet('x3');
    }
  }

  loading();

  return {
    aboveTheFoldLoaded:         aboveTheFoldLoaded,
    atfLoadedForAJAXRequest:    atfLoadedForAJAXRequest,
    functionalLoaded:           functionalLoaded,
    fnLoadedForAJAXRequest:     fnLoadedForAJAXRequest,
    cfLoadedForAJAXRequest:     cfLoadedForAJAXRequest,
    criticalFeatureLoaded:      criticalFeatureLoaded,
    x1Loaded:                   x1Loaded,
    getScope:                   getScope,
    pageLoadedForAJAXRequest:   pageLoadedForAJAXRequest,
    resetUEForAJAXRequest:      resetUEForAJAXRequest,
    setIDForAJAXRequest:        setIDForAJAXRequest,
    setStartTimeForAJAXRequest: setStartTimeForAJAXRequest,
    x1LoadedForAJAXRequest:     x1LoadedForAJAXRequest,
    x2Loaded:                   x2Loaded,
    x2LoadedForAJAXRequest:     x2LoadedForAJAXRequest,
    x3Loaded:                   x3Loaded,
    x3LoadedForAJAXRequest:     x3LoadedForAJAXRequest,
  };
})();
</script>

  function buildIssInitObject(opts, issOpts, isNewIss) {
    var issInitObj = {
        src: opts.host
      , sessionId: opts.sessionId
      , requestId: opts.requestId
      , mkt: opts.marketId
      , obfMkt: opts.obfuscatedMarketId
      , pageType: opts.pageType

      , fresh: opts.fresh
      , b2b: opts.b2b
      , aliases: opts.searchAliases

      , isDigitalFeaturesEnabled: issOpts.isDigitalFeaturesEnabled
      , isWayfindingEnabled: issOpts.isWayfindingEnabled
      , issPrimeEligible: issOpts.issPrimeEligible
      , deptText: issOpts.departmentText
      , sugText: issOpts.suggestionText
      , filterAliases: opts.filterAliases
      , biaWidgetUrl: opts.biaWidgetUrl
      , recentSearchesTreatment: issOpts.recentSearchesTreatment
      , authorSuggestionText: issOpts.authorSuggestionText
      , translatedStringsMap: issOpts.translatedStringsMap
      , biaTitleText: issOpts.biaTitleText
      , biaPurchasedText: issOpts.biaPurchasedText
      , biaViewAllText: issOpts.biaViewAllText
      , biaViewAllManageText: issOpts.biaViewAllManageText
      , biaAndText: issOpts.biaAndText
      , biaManageText: issOpts.biaManageText
      , biaWeblabTreatment: issOpts.biaWeblabTreatment
      , issNavConfig: issOpts.issNavConfig
      , cf: issOpts.cf
      , ime: opts.isJpOrCn
      , mktid: opts.marketId
      , qs: opts.isJpOrCn
      , issCorpus: issOpts.issCorpus
      , deepNodeISS: {
          searchAliasAccessor: function($) {
            return (window.SearchPageAccess && window.SearchPageAccess.searchAlias()) ||
                   $('select.searchSelect').children().attr('data-root-alias');
          },
          searchAliasDisplayNameAccessor: function() {
            return (window.SearchPageAccess && window.SearchPageAccess.searchAliasDisplayName());
          }
        }
      , removeDeepNodeISS: issOpts.removeDeepNodeISS
      , trendingTreatment: issOpts.trendingTreatment
      , useAPIV2: issOpts.useAPIV2
      , opfSwitch: issOpts.opfSwitch
      , isISSDesktopRefactorEnabled: issOpts.isISSDesktopRefactorEnabled
      , disableNavConfigFetch: issOpts.disableNavConfigFetch
      , isAPICachingDisabled: issOpts.isAPICachingDisabled
      , isInternal: issOpts.isInternal
      , useServiceHighlighting: issOpts.useServiceHighlighting
    };

    // If we aren't using the new ISS then we need to add these properties
    if (!isNewIss) {
      issInitObj.dd = issOpts.dropdown; // The element with id searchDropdownBox doesn't exist in C.
      issInitObj.imeSpacing = issOpts.imeSpacing;
      issInitObj.isNavInline = 1;
      issInitObj.triggerISSOnClick = 0;
      issInitObj.sc = 1;
      issInitObj.np = issOpts.np;
    }

    return issInitObj;
  } // END buildIssInitObject

<div id="huc-checkout-prefetch" class="a-row">
  <input type="hidden" name="" value="/gp/cart/cas.html" id="cas-url">
  <input type="hidden" name="" value="/gp/remotepagelet/signin/checkout-perf-initiate-and-store.html" id="checkout-prefetch-url">
</div>





<script type="text/javascript">
P.when('ready').register('CheckoutPrefetch', function() {
  function firePrefetchRequest(prefetchUrl) {
    // Why we have to use iframe?
    var iframe = document.createElement("iframe");
    iframe.setAttribute("src", prefetchUrl);
    iframe.setAttribute("style", "width:0px;height:0px;display:none;position:absolute;");
    iframe.setAttribute("name", "checkoutPrefetch");

    // Why we insert into head?
    if (document.head) {
        document.head.appendChild (iframe);
    } else {
        document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0].appendChild (iframe);
    }
  }

  function initiateAndStorePurchase(initiateId) {
    var cartInitiateId = initiateId ? initiateId : new Date().getTime();

    var hucProceed = document.getElementById('hlb-ptc-btn');
    if (hucProceed) {
      var ptcBtn = hucProceed.getElementsByTagName('a');
      if (ptcBtn.length === 0) return;

      var href = ((ptcBtn[0]).href);
      if (href && href.indexOf('https') >= 0) {   // it's a valid signin url
        if (href.indexOf('?') > 0) {
          href += '&cartInitiateId=' + cartInitiateId;
        } else {
          href += '?cartInitiateId=' + cartInitiateId;
        }
        (ptcBtn[0]).setAttribute('href', href);
      }
    }

    // Add the iFrame, kicking off the initiate
    firePrefetchRequest("/gp/cart/checkout-prefetch.html?ie=UTF8&checkAuthentication=1&checkDefaults=1&isToBeGiftWrapped=0&cartInitiateId=" + cartInitiateId);
  }

  function clearInitiateIdInLink(href) {
    // clear the id like uri?xxx=111&cartInitiateId=123123..
    var re = /&cartInitiateId=\d*/;
    if (re.test(href)) {
      return href.replace(/&cartInitiateId=\d*/, '');
    }

    // clear the id like uri?cartInitiateId=123123&xxx=111..
    re = /\?cartInitiateId=\d*&/;
    if (re.test(href)) {
      return href.replace(/cartInitiateId=\d*&/, '');
    }

    // clear the id like uri?cartInitiateId=123123
    re = /\?cartInitiateId=\d*/;
    if (re.test(href)) {
      return href.replace(/\?cartInitiateId=\d*/, '');
    }
    return href;
  }

  //function to clear params "&cartInitiateId=xxx"in PTC link
  //it depends on A and jQuery as they are both ready when invoking this func
  function clearHUCPTCInitiateId() {
    P.when('A', 'jQuery').execute(function(A, $) {
      var hucProceed = $('span.hlb-checkout-button a');
      if (hucProceed.length > 0) {
        var href = hucProceed.attr('href');
        if (href.indexOf('https') >= 0) {
          href = clearInitiateIdInLink(href);
          hucProceed.attr('href', href);
        }
      }
    });
  }

  P.when('ready').execute(function() {
    firePrefetchRequest("/gp/buy/prefetch/pipeline-assets.html");
  });
  initiateAndStorePurchase();

  return {
    initiateAndStorePurchase: initiateAndStorePurchase,
    clearHUCPTCInitiateId:    clearHUCPTCInitiateId
  }
});
</script>
